In particular, it must not\n    52→// be a null pointer.  null pointers are pre-filtered and never\n    53→// inserted into a SATB buffer.\n    54→//\n    55→// An entry that is below the TAMS pointer for the containing heap\n    56→// region requires marking. Such an entry must point to a valid object.\n    57→//\n    58→// An entry that is at least the TAMS pointer for the containing heap\n    59→// region might be any of the following, none of which should be marked.\n    60→//\n    61→// * A reference to an object allocated since marking started.\n    62→//   According to SATB, such objects are implicitly kept live and do\n    63→//   not need to be dealt with via SATB buffer processing.\n    64→//\n    65→// * A reference to a young generation object. Young objects are\n    66→//   handled separately and are not marked by concurrent marking.\n    67→//\n    68→// * A stale reference to a young generation object. potentially expensive operation, decrease the\n  // limits to get the regular clock call early\n  decrease_limits();\n}\n\nvoid G1CMTask::clear_mark_stats_cache(uint region_idx) {\n  _mark_stats_cache.reset(region_idx);\n}\n\nPair<size_t, size_t> G1CMTask::flush_mark_stats_cache() {\n  return _mark_stats_cache.evict_all();\n}\n\nvoid G1CMTask::print_stats() {\n  log_debug(gc, stats)(\"Marking Stats, task = %u, calls = %u\", _worker_id, _calls);\n  log_debug(gc, stats)(\"  Elapsed time = %1.2lfms, Termination time = %1.2lfms\",\n                       _elapsed_time_ms,               _step_times_ms.avg(),\n                       _step_times_ms.sd(),\n                       _step_times_ms.maximum(),\n                       _step_times_ms.sum());\n  size_t const hits = _mark_stats_cache.hits();\n  size_t const misses = _mark_stats_cache.misses();\n  log_debug(gc, stats)(\"  Mark Stats Cache: hits %zu misses %zu ratio %.3f\",\n                       hits, misses, percent_of(hits, hits + misses));\n}\n\nbool G1ConcurrentMark::try_stealing(uint worker_id, G1TaskQueueEntry& task_entry) {\n  return _task_queues->steal(worker_id, task_entry);\n}\n\nvoid G1CMTask::process_current_region(G1CMBitMapClosure& bitmap_closure) {\n  if (has_aborted() || _curr_region == nullptr) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // This means that we're already holding on to a region.\n  assert(_finger != nullptr, \"if region is not null, then the finger \"\n         \"should not be null either\");\n\n  // We might have restarted this task after an evacuation pause\n  // which might have evacuated the region we're holding on to\n  // underneath our feet. Let's read its limit again to make sure\n  // that we do not iterate over a region of the heap that\n  // contains garbage (update_region_limit() will also move\n  // _finger to the start of the region if it is found empty).\n  update_region_limit();\n  // We will start from _finger not from the start of the region,\n  // as we might be restarting this task after aborting half-way\n  // through scanning this region. In this case, _finger points to\n  // the address where we last found a marked object. If this is a\n  // fresh region, _finger points to start().\n  MemRegion mr = MemRegion(_finger, _region_limit);\n\n  assert(!_curr_region->is_humongous() || mr.start() == _curr_region->bottom(),\n         \"humongous regions should go around loop once only\");\n\n  // Some special cases:\n  // If the memory region is empty, we can just give up the region.\n  // If the current region is humongous then we only need to check\n  // the bitmap for the bit associated with the start of the object,\n  // scan the object if it's live, and give up the region.\n  // Otherwise, let's iterate over the bitmap of the part of the region\n  // that is left.\n  // If the iteration is successful, give up the region.\n  if (mr.is_empty()) {\n    giveup_current_region();\n    abort_marking_if_regular_check_fail();\n  } else if (_curr_region->is_humongous() && mr.start() == _curr_region->bottom()) {\n    if (_mark_bitmap->is_marked(mr.start())) {","numLines":100,"startLine":2424,"totalLines":3189}}}

Here are the key components and how they interact:\\n\\n## G1ConcurrentMark Start Trigger\\n\\nThe concurrent marking cycle is initiated based on heap occupancy thresholds. The **g1IHOPControl.hpp/cpp** files implement the IHOP (Initiating Heap Occupancy Percent) control, which calculates `get_conc_mark_start_threshold()` to determine when marking should start. The **g1Policy.hpp/cpp** monitors heap occupancy and calls `initiate_conc_mark()` when the IHOP threshold is reached. This triggers a concurrent start pause in **g1CollectedHeap.cpp** which calls `concurrent_cycle_start()` in **g1ConcurrentMark.cpp**.\\n\\n## Concurrent Marking Cycle Orchestration\\n\\nThe **g1ConcurrentMarkThread.hpp/cpp** manages the entire marking cycle through phases defined in `concurrent_mark_cycle_do()`. The cycle progresses through:\\n\\n1. **Root Region Scanning** (`phase_scan_root_regions`): Scans regions containing strong references to young objects\\n2. **Concurrent Mark Loop** (`phase_mark_loop`): The main marking phase executed by worker threads\\n3. **Rebuild and Scrub** (`phase_rebuild_and_scrub`): Rebuilds remembered sets after marking\\n4. **Cleanup Pause** (`phase_cleanup`): Final cleanup including collection set selection\\n\\nThe `concurrent_cycle_start()` method in **g1ConcurrentMark.cpp** initializes the marking cycle, while `post_concurrent_mark_start()` sets up concurrent marking parameters.\\n\\n## SATB Marking Queue Processing\\n\\nThe **g1SATBMarkQueueSet.hpp/cpp** manages the Snapshot-At-The-Beginning (SATB) buffers where references are recorded during concurrent marking. The `filter()` method in **g1SATBMarkQueueSet.cpp** determines which entries in SATB buffers require marking by checking if objects were allocated before marking started and whether they're already marked.\\n\\nDuring concurrent marking, **g1ConcurrentMark.cpp** contains the critical `drain_satb_buffers()` method (line 2424) called by G1CMTask workers. This method iterates through completed SATB buffers using `G1CMSATBBufferClosure` and applies marking to the entries. The remark phase finalizes SATB processing through `finalize_marking()` and the **G1CMRemarkTask** which processes remaining buffers.\\n\\n## Concurrent Marking Worker Tasks\\n\\nThe marking work is distributed via worker tasks:\\n\\n- **G1CMConcurrentMarkingTask** (line 976 in g1ConcurrentMark.cpp): Runs concurrent marking, where each worker executes G1CMTask instances calling `do_marking_step()` which performs object scanning and SATB buffer draining\\n- **G1CMRemarkTask** (line 1829 in g1ConcurrentMark.cpp): Handles the remark pause when concurrent marking must be finalized\\n- **G1CMTask**: The core marking worker that scans marked objects, processes the mark stack, and drains SATB buffers\\n\\n## Remembered Set Scanning\\n\\nAfter concurrent marking completes, the **g1RemSet.hpp/cpp** and **g1HeapRegionRemSet.hpp/cpp** manage remembered set scanning. The `scan_heap_roots()` method in **g1RemSet.cpp** is called during evacuation phases to identify references from non-collected regions into the collection set. Each region maintains a **G1HeapRegionRemSet** that tracks references from other regions via card-based tracking.\\n\\n## Mixed Collection Region Selection\\n\\nAfter marking completes, **g1CollectionSetChooser.cpp** selects old generation regions for the mixed collection phases. The `G1CollectionSetChooser::build()` method (line 262) constructs collection set candidates by:\\n\\n1. Spawning **G1BuildCandidateRegionsTask** workers to analyze all old regions\\n2. Calculating garbage collection efficiency for each region based on live bytes and remembered set occupancy\\n3. Filtering regions based on the `mixed_gc_live_threshold_bytes()` threshold\\n\\nThe selected regions are stored in **g1CollectionSetCandidates.hpp/cpp** and used by the young collector to schedule mixed evacuations until sufficient space is reclaimed.\\n\\n## Integration Point\\n\\nThe cycle completes when `concurrent_cycle_end()` is called in both **g1ConcurrentMarkThread.cpp** and **g1ConcurrentMark.cpp**, which updates completion counters and cleanup state.
